The snowflake crisp gift box in the room was already prepared, and the fruits were very good. Xiao Luo was also very considerate. He helped us apply for a river view room and connected the two rooms. The communication between the two rooms was very smooth. The river view room has a very good view. I recommend it to everyone. The only point that needs to be improved is that the time on the clock in the room is not right. I hope the people at houseKeepin can adjust it in time. In addition, the drainage of the sink is a bit slow. When the faucet is turned on, all the accumulated water cannot be drained in time. I hope this problem can be solved. The water from the shower is very fast. I like the bathroom bathtub in the room very much.

posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:The location is very good, located at the intersection of Yongjiang River, Yuyao River and Fenghua River, which is convenient for travel. The hotel is very close to Jiangxia Bridge East and East Gate on Line 1, and can be reached in about 10 minutes on foot. It is very convenient to get there. The East Gate subway station is Tianyi Square, which has a strong commercial a**osphere and is fully equipped with food, drink and entertainment. The hotel service is very good, the sanitation is very clean, the room glass is also very clean, and the view is wide. Insufficient, it is recommended that the hotel improve: 
1. The road construction at the entrance of the hotel, the navigation usually leads to the entrance of Yangliu Street, but this road is very narrow, and it will be a bit nervous when two cars meet. It will be more relaxed to enter from the Baizhang Road entrance. It is recommended that the hotel have a prompt at the entrance of Yangliu Street. 
2. The hotel room is equipped with a charging cable, but the speed is very slow, there are very few sockets on both ends, all are three-pin sockets, and there are very few sockets that can be plugged into the mobile phone plug, which is very inconvenient. 
3. There are DVDs from the last century in the room, which is really meaningless. It is better to improve the charging facilities. 
4. There is a bed in the room, but it cannot be opened. It depends on air conditioning for ventilation. The carpet still has a bit of smell. 
5. The breakfast coffee machine did not work properly for three consecutive days. The waiter had to make coffee in the backstage.
6. I booked three nights, which included breakfast for two adults every day for three days. There was no problem on the first two days, but on the third day, the waiter said there was only breakfast for one person. I don't know why. There was no problem on the first two days, but it didn't work on the third day. Although it was properly resolved, as a five-star hotel, such a mistake is puzzling.

Coupled with the colorful and cute muddy theme of the bedroom, we really didn‚Äôt want to go to bed until 10:00 at night and wanted to play some more.
This is not the point between the rooms that I think is outstanding. I think the most important part is that this room really has a lot of thoughtful details for the children. For example, there are play facilities in the room, such as footstools for children, slippers for children, bathrobes for children, and even bath toys and bath seats for children. Every time we travel and stay in a hotel with Coca-Cola, we are actually very tired when we bathe the children in the bathtub. The first reason is because there is no place for parents to sit down, and the second reason is that the children are in the bathtub and they are really tired. It is easy to slip and fall. Even using the hotel's anti-slip mat is very dangerous, because the area where children can move will be much larger than that of the anti-slip store. But this time when we checked in, the room provided a bathing seat. Sitting in the seat firstly secures the child, and secondly, he will not slip when he stands up. In addition, with the company of bath toys, and the child's step stool, parents can sit by the bathtub. Taking a shower really frees up my old mother's waist. These facilities can really help parents relax while traveling. There is also a singing night light in the bedroom. Children will feel a little uneasy when sleeping in a new environment. Put on the night light and turn on the light to shine on the ceiling. The children will slowly relax. I think this design Also very considerate.
Finally, I have to say that the buffet breakfast really satisfies the traditional taste buds of Ningbo people. There are rice cakes, tofu curd, noodles, fried dumplings, and even glutinous rice balls for eating early in the morning! Even if I have a stomach for Western food, I can enjoy the meal as there are freshly baked desserts and croissants in the morning. You can also refresh yourself with a latte!
In addition, there is a large amusement park outside the restaurant, and the children can't move there until it rains in the past two days, so there is no place to play outdoors. Inside the hotel, I didn't expect that the children can play Completely released! I really like this hotel and this family room. Next time I have a vacation, I can bring my kids here to relax and relax by myselfü•≥ü•≥ü•≥
